Chapter 2 More exploration on progenitors

Idents(data_seurat) <- 'Type_step1'
data_sub <- subset(data_seurat, idents = 'Progenitor')
data_sub <- CreateSeuratObject(counts = data_sub@assays$RNA@counts,
                               meta.data = data_sub@meta.data,
                               min.cells = 3)
dim(data_sub)
## [1] 16180  5280
# scale data before clustering
data_sub <- NormalizeData(object = data_sub, normalization.method = "LogNormalize", scale.factor = 1e4)
data_sub <- ScaleData(data_sub)
#data_sub <- ScaleData(data_sub, vars.to.regress = c("pct_counts_MT", "gender"))
data_sub <- FindVariableFeatures(data_sub, selection.method = "vst", nfeatures = 2000)
top <- head(VariableFeatures(data_sub), 30)
plot1 <- VariableFeaturePlot(data_sub)
plot2 <- LabelPoints(plot = plot1, points = top, repel = TRUE)
plot2

2.1 PCA on Progenitors

2.1.1 Genes associated with each PC

data_sub <- RunPCA(data_sub, features = VariableFeatures(object = data_sub), npcs = 50)
ElbowPlot(data_sub, ndims = 50, reduction = 'pca')

viz <- VizDimLoadings(
                      data_sub,
                      dims = 1:50,
                      nfeatures = 40,
                      col = "blue",
                      reduction = "pca",
                      projected = FALSE,
                      balanced = FALSE,
                      combine = FALSE
)
print(data_sub[["pca"]], dims = 1:50, nfeatures = 100)

2.1.2 Metadata associated with each PC

data_sce <- as.SingleCellExperiment(data_sub)
pca_stdev <- data_sub@reductions$pca@stdev
plotReducedDim(data_sce,
               dimred = "PCA",
               ncomponents = 3,
               percentVar = pca_stdev,
               colour_by= "Phase",
               point_alpha = 0.5,
               point_size = 0.1)

plotReducedDim(data_sce,
               dimred = "PCA",
               ncomponents = c(3,6,7),
               percentVar = pca_stdev,
               colour_by= "Phase",
               point_alpha = 0.5,
               point_size = 0.1)
